              SAN Tourism Software Group providing Software Solutions for Incoming Travel Agencies as well as Tour Operators since 1992. Our brands are used by more than 500 business partners in 70 countries and 4 continents. 

Sejourâ„¢ Incoming Agency Software, has been developed together with the experiences acquiring by the Tourism Sector since 1992, With this single software Reservation, Contracting, Operation, Invoicing, Tour, Current Accounts menus are working online with a modular logic.

TourVisioâ„¢ Tour Operator Software, enables entry of all kind of service contracts, considering their special offers it can generate dynamic packages on purpose per different markets. Price lists and catalogues can be laid out easily. Flexible profit margin definitions enables you to determine your sales strategies for different packages or individual tours faster and with ease, automatically new price lists are being generated according to the price modifications. Enables to sell all types of services and their sub-products to the end users. Optimization module enables agents to reach the most accurate flight and hotel availability information and helping them to find the best travel solution to their clients, flight and hotel availability can be searched at the same time or separately as preferred.
